</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   Should you tire of adventure or seek a peaceful nights rest, the Grunting
Boar Inn is willing to accommodate any traveler that carry enough gold.  The

</font><font color="#00FFFF">The Temple of Midgaard
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   Entering the great halls of the Temple of Midgaard is awe-inspiring, as you
stand at an ornate entryway spanning nearly thirty feet across.  Huge copper
braziers at each temple corner bathes the cool, marble walls in a fiery glow.  
Elaborate tapestries bearing the crests and symbols of nobles who helped
established the Temple long ago hang gracefully from the walls and ceilings.  A
set of large stone steps inside the temple lead up to an altar dedicated to the
heroes and patrons of this age.  The entire temple is elevated prominently above
all the other buildings of Midgaard, reinforcing its position as the pinnacle
landmark within the city.

is built within the Grand Gates of the Temple.  The gates are gargantuan in

</font><font color="#00FFFF">The Temple of Midgaard
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   Entering the great halls of the Temple of Midgaard is awe-inspiring, as you
stand at an ornate entryway spanning nearly thirty feet across.  Huge copper
braziers at each temple corner bathes the cool, marble walls in a fiery glow.  
Elaborate tapestries bearing the crests and symbols of nobles who helped
established the Temple long ago hang gracefully from the walls and ceilings.  A
set of large stone steps inside the temple lead up to an altar dedicated to the
heroes and patrons of this age.  The entire temple is elevated prominently above
all the other buildings of Midgaard, reinforcing its position as the pinnacle
landmark within the city.

</font><font color="#00FFFF">The Temple of Midgaard
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   Entering the great halls of the Temple of Midgaard is awe-inspiring, as you
stand at an ornate entryway spanning nearly thirty feet across.  Huge copper
braziers at each temple corner bathes the cool, marble walls in a fiery glow.  
Elaborate tapestries bearing the crests and symbols of nobles who helped
established the Temple long ago hang gracefully from the walls and ceilings.  A
set of large stone steps inside the temple lead up to an altar dedicated to the
heroes and patrons of this age.  The entire temple is elevated prominently above
all the other buildings of Midgaard, reinforcing its position as the pinnacle
landmark within the city.

</font><font color="#00FFFF">Market Square
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   You are standing on the Market Square, the famous Square of Midgaard.  It is
said that the North, East, South, and West all meet here.  This square is the
busiest in the realms for Midgaard is the center of the known civilization.

square.  Roads lead in every direction, north to the temple square, south to
the bazaar, east and west bound is the main street.

</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   The arched entrance to the spire opens up to you from the street to the east.

from a single great tree.

</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   You are by two large towers that have been built into the city wall.

</font><font color="#00FFFF">The Magic Shop
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   Stepping inside the Magic Shop is like crossing the boundaries of an optical
illusion, as the immediate impression is the interior of the shop is many times
larger than the outside might suggest.  No doubt powerful magical spells are
being used effectively to provide the real estate, as rows and rows of various
items are stacked haphazardly in shelves as far as the eye can see.  Potions,
scrolls, and various odds and ends that are used for magical arts are available
for sale here.  Anyone even thinking of shoplifting might be forewarned, the
shop items are guarded with deadly protective runes that have disabled many a
would-be thief.

</font><font color="#00FFFF">Inside the West Gate of Midgaard
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   You are by two large towers that have been built into the city wall.  
Connecting the towers high up in the air is a narrow walkway that the guards use
to cross from one tower to the next.  Between the towers is a heavy iron gate
that is used to keep the enemies of Midgaard out.  Along the top of the towers,
huge magical fires burn providing a bright light even on the darkest of the
nights.
   Main Street begins to the east, Wall Road begins to the south, and to
the north a small dirt path runs along the side of the wall.  As far as
beyond the gate, gently rolling hills converge with river and forest.

</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   You are at the northern end of Wall Road.  Farther to north you can see the
Western Gate of Midgaard.  The street is quite busy for it is a popular route
taken by travelers to enter the Southern Midgaard.  From the tall city wall
that runs parallel to the road along its western edge, it is quite easy to
figure out where the name for this street came from.  Along the street can be
found tall poles with magical lanterns, provided by the sorcerer's guild, that
glow with a bright light when it gets dark.  The street continues south towards

</font><font color="#00FFFF">Market Square
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   You are standing on the Market Square, the famous Square of Midgaard.  It is
said that the North, East, South, and West all meet here.  This square is the
busiest in the realms for Midgaard is the center of the known civilization.  
People from all lands can be found wandering here.  At the four corners can be
found tall poles with magical lanterns, provided by the Mage's Guild, that glow
with a bright light when it gets dark.  
   A large fountain of an angel pouring water stands in the center of the
square.  Roads lead in every direction, north to the temple square, south to
the bazaar, east and west bound is the main street.
